CHRONOLOGICAL LISTING

There are break points in this listing which is in five parts:

700 - 1500
1501 - 1660
1661 - 1720
1721 - 1800
1801 - 1824
1825 - 1850

Use your browser's find function to locate the start of a new section.
This is a name and place listing without notes.
This is a large file!
A large number of libraries are of uncertain date of foundation.
